get_current_board


## ExplanationNote that in this setup the initial game state is not provided in the query, making it impossible to evaluate legal moves or select a UCI continuation without first retrieving the position. The action get_current_board therefore serves as the required information-gathering step, allowing inspection of the current FEN, piece placement, castling rights, en-passant status, and whose turn it is before any subsequent get_legal_moves or make_move call. This follows the enumerated action protocol exactly while preserving the ability to act as Black on the subsequent turn.
